# ATM Error Codes

Generated from `packages/`, `scripts/`, `tests`, and `examples` TypeScript sources plus `docs/governance/error-code-registry.json`.

Regenerate with `npm run generate:error-codes`.

## Operator Registry

Curated entries provide the shared operator-facing meaning and recovery path used by ATM skills. Source-scanned codes that are not yet curated appear as `registry-missing` in the source index.

| Code | Category | Description | Retryable | Human Approval | Remediation | Source Owner |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `ATM_GIT_COMMIT_BRANCH_QUEUE_BUSY` | git-governance | Another governed commit is currently finalizing the same branch. | yes | no | - Run node atm.mjs git commit-status --actor &lt;actor&gt; --json to inspect the branchCommitQueueStatus owner and age.&lt;br&gt;- If the owner is alive, wait for it to finish and retry the same governed commit command.&lt;br&gt;- If the owner is stale or dead, inspect the lock path and current HEAD before cleaning it through the governed recovery lane. | `packages/cli/src/commands/git-governance.ts` |
| `ATM_GIT_COMMIT_BROKER_CONFLICT_OVERRIDE_REQUIRED` | team-broker | A Team Broker ownership conflict blocks commit bypass until a recorded conflict-resolution artifact and approval exist. | yes | yes | - Resolve the ownership conflict through a paper-style broker conflict-resolution artifact.&lt;br&gt;- Obtain the required backend.brokerConflictOverride approval only when a human has approved the override.&lt;br&gt;- Retry the governed commit with --broker-conflict-resolution and the approved lease. | `packages/cli/src/commands/git-governance.ts` |
| `ATM_GIT_COMMIT_STDIN_PATHSPEC_ADD_ACTIVE` | git-governance | A git add helper using stdin pathspecs is active and can make a governed commit appear hung. | yes | no | - Run node atm.mjs git commit-status --actor &lt;actor&gt; --json and inspect stdinPathspecGitAddProcesses.&lt;br&gt;- Wait briefly for the listed helper to finish, or terminate only the listed stuck git add process after confirming it is the stdin pathspec helper.&lt;br&gt;- Manual staging with git add -- &lt;paths&gt; is normal and safe when the path list is finite and reviewed.&lt;br&gt;- For governed scoped delivery, prefer node atm.mjs git commit --auto-stage; ATM auto-stage uses explicit git add -- &lt;paths&gt; and does not use stdin pathspec staging. | `packages/cli/src/commands/git-governance.ts` |
| `ATM_GIT_COMMIT_STDIN_PATHSPEC_ADD_CLEAR` | git-governance | No active stdin pathspec git add helper is currently visible to ATM commit-status. | yes | no | - Proceed with explicit staging or the governed ATM auto-stage lane.&lt;br&gt;- If the UI still appears stuck, inspect the branch commit queue and recent commit attempt status before retrying. | `packages/cli/src/commands/git-governance.ts` |
| `ATM_NEXT_TASK_SCOPE_NOT_FOUND` | routing | ATM could not match the prompt to an imported task card or ledger task. | yes | no | - If authoring a new task, create or update the planning card first.&lt;br&gt;- Dry-run import the planning card with node atm.mjs tasks import --from &lt;card&gt; --dry-run --json.&lt;br&gt;- When the dry run is clean, import with --write and commit the ledger import bundle before claiming implementation. | `packages/cli/src/commands/next.ts` |
| `ATM_RUNNER_SYNC_REQUIRED` | runner-mode | The frozen ATM runner is older than source changes and must be rebuilt before frozen-runner validation is trusted. | yes | no | - Run ATM_RETAIN_RELEASE_ARTIFACTS=1 npm run build from the framework repository.&lt;br&gt;- Rerun the same node atm.mjs command after the build and confirm runnerMode.sourceDrift.syncRequired is false. | `packages/cli/src/commands/runner-mode` |
| `ATM_TASKS_AUDIT_WARNINGS` | task-ledger | Task audit passed but found active warnings that should be reviewed before claiming a clean ledger. | yes | no | - Read activeFindings in the tasks audit JSON output.&lt;br&gt;- Do not treat advisory output as a blocker unless the active task depends on the warned evidence.&lt;br&gt;- Open a repair or import follow-up when the warning is in the current delivery path. | `packages/cli/src/commands/tasks` |

## Registry Coverage

- Source-scanned ATM codes: 1335
- Curated registry entries: 7
- Registry-missing source codes: 1328

When a user-visible code is `registry-missing`, add or update one entry in `docs/governance/error-code-registry.json`, then rerun `npm run generate:error-codes`.
